 aajkal pairon kii sehat or sundarataa banaae rakhane ke liye log fish pedicor kii taraf zyada aakarshith ho rahe hai
 Fish pedicure is a type of therapy
 jisamen pairon ko machhliyon se bhare ek tub main daalaa jaataa he
 Small fishes in the tub separate the dead skin from your feet and eat it
 fish pedicor ke phaayde--fish pedicor karwaane se pairon kii skin mulaayam banati he
 - By getting a fish pedicure, you get relief from foot pain
 -fish pedicor karwaane se eczema or psoriasis jaisi bimariyon main phayda hota he
 You will not have to put too much emphasis on your pocket to get a fish pedicure done
 bataa den, yah bahut zyada manhagaa bhi nahin hota he
 -fishes used for pedicure cleanse dead skin and increase the blood flow of the body
 - pedicor karne vaali gaara rupha naam kii machhliyaan pairon kii ded skin ko khaakar unhen sundar or gloing banane main madad karti hai
 Disadvantages of fish pedicures - Many times you have seen people in malls or parlors getting their pedicures done by putting their feet in the same tank
 lekin kya aap jaanate hai aapkaa aisa karnaa aapke liye sehat ke liye kitna surakshit he
 Fish pedicures are safe only when cleanliness is taken care of while getting them done
 gaara rupha naam kii machhliyaan fish pedicor karne ke liye istemaal kii jaati he
 Women should pay attention to these important things while getting a fish pedicure
 varanaa iskaa asar aapaki sehat par pad saktaa he
 Let's know what should be kept in mind while getting a fish pedicure
 -kai baar fish pedicor karne vaale parlor or spa centre ke log tub ke pani ko kai dinon tak nahin badalte
 Because of this, you may have a variety of skin infections due to mycobacteria present in the tank
 fish pedicor karavaate samay is baat kaa dhyaan rakhen ki tub kaa pani roj badla jaataa or pani saaf ho
 Keep in mind that if the spa people do not change the tub water after doing a fish pedicure, the risk of infection increases
 saavdhaaniyaan--agar aapke pairon main chot lagi ho to fish pedicor na karavaaen
 By doing this, bleeding starts from the injury while doing the pedicure
 jo tub main jaakar infections kaa kaaran banataa he
 -if you start having sudden bleeding from your feet while taking a fish pedicure, clean your feet immediately with any antiseptic medicine by taking them out of the water immediately
 -agar aap pehle se hi kisi shaareerik samasya yaa chot se jujh rahe hai to bhuulakar bhi fish pedicor karwaane kii galati na karen

 peedita kii maane to phone automobile kaarobaari nikhil priyadarshi kaa tha

 jiske baad nikhil use lagaataar phone karne laga or usne peedita se dosti karne kii baat kahi

 phone par baatcheet badhati gai or aae din donon ghar se baahar milane lage

 ek din nikhil range rover car lekar peedita se milane aayaa or usne peedita ko prapoj kiya

 peedita kisi tarah vahaan se nikalne main kaamyaab rahi

 When there is a ruckus about loudspeakers ringing at religious places in the country, a Muslim personality has come forward in Mumbai who has been openly and consistently opposing the movement on loudspeakers despite being a Muslim
 mumbai ke mohammad ali urf babubhai 66 saal ke namaji musalmaan hai or laudspikar se di hui ajaan ko gaiyr islamic maanate hai
 In order to get his point across, he put a petition in the High Court
 paise kam the isliye maamle main pairvi khud kii or sabit kiya ki quran ko laudspikar kii azaan ganvaara nahin
 In an exclusive conversation with NDTV, petitioner Mohammad Ali alias Babubhai said that the use of loudspeakers is not a part of religion
 na hi yah buniyadi he
 Because religion is 1400 years old and loudspeakers have arrived just a few hundred years ago
 laudspikar ko hataanaa dharm ko koi khatra nahin he
 Religion is complete in itself
 wo langadaa nahin he ki use laudspikar kii baisakhi dekar taqatvar banaao
 Babu Bhai's legal victory has now turned into a campaign
 unhone apane daawey ko majboot banane ke liye dharmagranth ke saath maulaviyon ke 64 fatve bhi dhund nikaale hai
 He constantly states that his fight is not against religion but against the extra and unnecessary things added to everyday conduct in the name of religion
 quran ke hawaale se unhone mumbai main beharam paada or bharat nagar jaise muslim bahul ilaakon kii saat masjidon par se saare bhompu utarava die hai
 It took time for the fighters to gather courage
 sthaneey madani masjid ke trustee mohammad nazar ne NDTV india ko bataaya ki unki masjid main teen spikar lage hue the
 They were not removed simultaneously but slowly
 pehle azaan main phir namaaj main or jumme main ise hataa diya
 The comments dharmasthalon par bajte laudspikar ko lekar santosh pachalag, dow bedekar or mohammad ali teenon kii yachikaaon par ek saath sunwaayee karte hue bambai hoicourt ke justise ok or justise syed amjad ne agast 2016 main faisla sunaate hue kaha ki desh me kahin bhi laudspikar kaa istemaal raat das se subah 6 ke bich karne waalon par ek lakh rupee tak kaa jurmaana or paanch saal tak kii jail hogi
 Significantly, Babubhai used constitutional rights instead of speaking on social media to make his point
 is vajah se aayaa faisla ab puure desh par lagu ho chukaa he

 unki ladaai main saath dene waalon ko himmat jutaney main bhi vakt laga
 Mohammad Nazar, a trustee of the local Madni mosque, told NDTV India that there were three speakers in his mosque
 inhen ek saath nahin balki dhire-dhire hataaya

 tippaniyan Hearing together the petitions of Santosh Pachalag, Dr
 Bedekar and Mohammad Ali three, regarding the loudspeakers ringing at the shrines, Justice Oak and Justice Syed Amjad of the Bombay High Court ruled in August 2016 that loudspeakers can be used anywhere in the country at night
 Those doing between 6 am to 6 am will be fined up to Rs 1 lakh and imprisoned for up to five years
 gauratlab he ki babubhai ne apni baat rakhane ke liye soshal media par bolne ke bajaae sanvaidhanik haq kaa istemaal kiya
